00001: # deploy-all-agents.ps1
00002: Write-Host "=== DEPLOIEMENT COMPLET DES 9 AGENTS ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00003: Write-Host "Date: $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')" -ForegroundColor Gray
00004: Write-Host ""
00005: 
00006: $projectPath = "$env:USERPROFILE\Projects\SmartContractPipeline"
00007: if (-not (Test-Path $projectPath)) {
00008:     Write-Host "Création du dossier projet..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00009:     New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $projectPath -Force | Out-Null
00010: }
00011: 
00012: Set-Location $projectPath
00013: 
00014: # 1. Créer la structure complète des agents
00015: Write-Host "1. CREATION DE LA STRUCTURE DES AGENTS..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00016: $agentsStructure = @{
00017:     "agents/architect" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py")
00018:     "agents/coder" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py")
00019:     "agents/communication" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "message_bus.py", "event_system.py")
00020:     "agents/documenter" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py")
00021:     "agents/formal_verification" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py")
00022:     "agents/frontend_web3" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py", "web3_hooks.py")
00023:     "agents/fuzzing_simulation" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py", "simulator.py")
00024:     "agents/quality_metrics" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py", "metrics.py")
00025:     "agents/smart_contract" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py", "security.py")
00026:     "agents/tester" = @("config.yaml", "agent.py", "tools.py", "test_generator.py")
00027:     "agents/orchestrator" = @("orchestrator.py", "task_manager.py", "state_manager.py")
00028:     "agents/shared" = @("base_agent.py", "memory.py", "context_manager.py")
00029: }
00030: 
00031: foreach ($folder in $agentsStructure.Keys) {
00032:     $fullPath = "$projectPath\$folder"
00033:     New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $fullPath -Force | Out-Null
00034:     
00035:     foreach ($file in $agentsStructure[$folder]) {
00036:         $filePath = "$fullPath\$file"
00037:         if (-not (Test-Path $filePath)) {
00038:             New-Item -ItemType File -Path $filePath -Force | Out-Null
00039:         }
00040:     }
00041:     Write-Host "   📁 $folder créé" -ForegroundColor Green
00042: }
00043: 
00044: # 2. Créer le fichier de versions
00045: Write-Host "`n2. CREATION DU FICHIER DE VERSIONS..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00046: $versions = @{
00047:     timestamp = Get-Date -Format "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"
00048:     system = @{
00049:         os = "Windows $( [System.Environment]::OSVersion.Version.ToString())"
00050:         powershell = $PSVersionTable.PSVersion.ToString()
00051:     }
00052:     tools = @{}
00053:     python = @{}
00054:     node = @{}
00055:     blockchain = @{}
00056:     agents = @{}
00057: }
00058: 
00059: # Récupérer les versions des outils
00060: try { $versions.tools.git = (git --version 2>&1).ToString().Replace('git version ', '').Trim() } catch { $versions.tools.git = "N/A" }
00061: try { $versions.tools.docker = (docker --version 2>&1).ToString().Replace('Docker version ', '').Split(',')[0].Trim() } catch { $versions.tools.docker = "N/A" }
00062: 
00063: # Récupérer les versions Python
00064: try { 
00065:     $pythonVersion = (python --version 2>&1).ToString().Replace('Python ', '').Trim()
00066:     $versions.python.version = $pythonVersion
00067:     
00068:     # Packages Python
00069:     $pythonPackages = @("langchain", "chromadb", "requests", "web3", "aiohttp")
00070:     foreach ($pkg in $pythonPackages) {
00071:         try {
00072:             $version = python -c "import $pkg; print(getattr($pkg, '__version__', 'N/A'))" 2>$null
00073:             if (-not $version -or $version -eq "N/A") {
00074:                 $version = pip show $pkg 2>$null | Select-String "Version:" | ForEach-Object { $_.ToString().Replace('Version: ', '').Trim() }
00075:             }
00076:             $versions.python.$pkg = $version
00077:         } catch {
00078:             $versions.python.$pkg = "N/A"
00079:         }
00080:     }
00081: } catch { $versions.python.version = "N/A" }
00082: 
00083: # Récupérer les versions Node.js
00084: try { 
00085:     $nodeVersion = (node --version 2>&1).ToString().Replace('v', '').Trim()
00086:     $versions.node.version = $nodeVersion
00087:     
00088:     # Packages Node.js globaux
00089:     $nodePackages = @("npm", "yarn", "hardhat", "typescript", "next")
00090:     foreach ($pkg in $nodePackages) {
00091:         try {
00092:             if ($pkg -eq "npm") {
00093:                 $version = (npm --version 2>&1).ToString().Trim()
00094:             } elseif ($pkg -eq "next") {
00095:                 $version = (npx next --version 2>&1).ToString().Trim()
00096:             } else {
00097:                 $version = (npx $pkg --version 2>&1).ToString().Trim()
00098:             }
00099:             $versions.node.$pkg = $version
00100:         } catch {
00101:             $versions.node.$pkg = "N/A"
00102:         }
00103:     }
00104: } catch { $versions.node.version = "N/A" }
00105: 
00106: # Récupérer les versions blockchain
00107: try { $versions.blockchain.foundry = (forge --version 2>&1 | Select-String "forge").ToString().Split(' ')[1].Trim() } catch { $versions.blockchain.foundry = "N/A" }
00108: try { $versions.blockchain.slither = (slither --version 2>&1).ToString().Trim() } catch { $versions.blockchain.slither = "N/A" }
00109: try { $versions.blockchain.anvil = (anvil --version 2>&1).ToString().Trim() } catch { $versions.blockchain.anvil = "N/A" }
00110: 
00111: # Sauvegarder les versions
00112: $versions | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 10 | Out-File -FilePath "$projectPath\config\versions.json" -Force
00113: Write-Host "   ✅ Fichier de versions créé" -ForegroundColor Green
00114: 
00115: # 3. Créer les configurations des agents
00116: Write-Host "`n3. CREATION DES CONFIGURATIONS D'AGENTS..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00117: 
00118: # Agent Architecte
00119: $architectConfig = @"
00120: # agents/architect/config.yaml
00121: agent_id: "architect_001"
00122: name: "Agent Architecte"
00123: version: "1.0.0"
00124: model: "ollama:deepseek-coder:6.7b"
00125: temperature: 0.3
00126: description: "Responsable de la conception architecturale du système"
00127: 
00128: tools:
00129:   - name: "diagram_generator"

00525: 
00526: # 4. Créer le base_agent.py (classe parente)
00527: Write-Host "`n4. CREATION DE LA CLASSE BASE AGENT..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00528: $baseAgentCode = @'
00529: # agents/shared/base_agent.py
00530: import asyncio
00531: import json
00532: import logging
00533: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
00534: from pathlib import Path
00535: from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
00536: import yaml
00537: 
00538: class BaseAgent(ABC):
00539:     """Classe de base pour tous les agents"""
00540:     
00541:     def __init__(self, config_path: str):
00542:         self.config = self._load_config(config_path)
00543:         self.agent_id = self.config.get("agent_id", "unknown")
00544:         self.name = self.config.get("name", "Unnamed Agent")
00545:         self.version = self.config.get("version", "1.0.0")
00546:         self.logger = self._setup_logger()
00547:         self.memory = {}
00548:         self.context = {}
00549:         
00550:     def _load_config(self, config_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00551:         """Charge la configuration YAML"""
00552:         try:
00553:             with open(config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00554:                 return yaml.safe_load(f)
00555:         except Exception as e:
00556:             print(f"Erreur lors du chargement de la configuration: {e}")
00557:             return {}
00558:     
00559:     def _setup_logger(self) -> logging.Logger:
00560:         """Configure le logger"""
00561:         logger = logging.getLogger(self.agent_id)
00562:         if not logger.handlers:
00563:             logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
00564:             handler = logging.StreamHandler()
00565:             formatter = logging.Formatter(
00566:                 f'%(asctime)s - {self.agent_id} - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00567:             )
00568:             handler.setFormatter(formatter)
00569:             logger.addHandler(handler)
00570:         return logger
00571:     
00572:     @abstractmethod
00573:     async def initialize(self) -> bool:
00574:         """Initialise l'agent"""
00575:         pass
00576:     
00577:     @abstractmethod
00578:     async def execute(self, task: Dict[str, Any], context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00579:         """Exécute une tâche"""
00580:         pass
00581:     
00582:     async def load_context(self, context_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00583:         """Charge le contexte depuis un fichier"""
00584:         try:
00585:             if Path(context_path).exists():
00586:                 with open(context_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00587:                     self.context = json.load(f)
00588:                     self.logger.info(f"Contexte chargé depuis {context_path}")
00589:                     return self.context
00590:         except Exception as e:
00591:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors du chargement du contexte: {e}")
00592:         return {}
00593:     
00594:     async def save_memory(self, memory_path: str) -> bool:
00595:         """Sauvegarde la mémoire de l'agent"""
00596:         try:
00597:             memory_dir = Path(memory_path).parent
00598:             memory_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00599:             
00600:             with open(memory_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00601:                 json.dump(self.memory, f, indent=2)
00602:             
00603:             self.logger.info(f"Mémoire sauvegardée dans {memory_path}")
00604:             return True
00605:         except Exception as e:
00606:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la sauvegarde de la mémoire: {e}")
00607:             return False
00608:     
00609:     def get_agent_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00610:         """Retourne les informations de l'agent"""
00611:         return {
00612:             "agent_id": self.agent_id,
00613:             "name": self.name,
00614:             "version": self.version,
00615:             "config": self.config,
00616:             "tools": self.config.get("tools", []),
00617:             "dependencies": self.config.get("dependencies", {})
00618:         }
00619:     
00620:     async def health_check(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00621:         """Vérifie la santé de l'agent"""
00622:         return {
00623:             "status": "healthy",
00624:             "agent_id": self.agent_id,
00625:             "timestamp": asyncio.get_event_loop().time(),
00626:             "memory_usage": len(str(self.memory)),
00627:             "context_loaded": bool(self.context)
00628:         }
00629: '@
00630: 
00631: $baseAgentCode | Out-File -FilePath "$projectPath\agents\shared\base_agent.py" -Force -Encoding UTF8
00632: 
00633: # 5. Créer l'orchestrateur principal
00634: Write-Host "`n5. CREATION DE L'ORCHESTRATEUR PRINCIPAL..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00635: $orchestratorCode = @'
00636: # agents/orchestrator/orchestrator.py
00637: import asyncio
00638: import json
00639: import yaml
00640: from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional
00641: from pathlib import Path
00642: import logging
00643: from datetime import datetime
00644: 
00645: class Orchestrator:
00646:     """Orchestrateur principal qui gère tous les agents"""
00647:     
00648:     def __init__(self, project_root: str = "."):
00649:         self.project_root = Path(project_root)
00650:         self.agents = {}
00651:         self.agent_status = {}
00652:         self.task_queue = asyncio.Queue()
00653:         self.results = {}
00654:         self.versions = self._load_versions()
00655:         
00656:         # Configuration
00657:         self.config = {
00658:             "max_concurrent_tasks": 3,
00659:             "task_timeout": 300,  # 5 minutes
00660:             "retry_attempts": 3
00661:         }
00662:         
00663:         self.logger = self._setup_logger()
00664:     
00665:     def _setup_logger(self) -> logging.Logger:
00666:         """Configure le logger"""
00667:         logger = logging.getLogger("orchestrator")
00668:         logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
00669:         
00670:         if not logger.handlers:
00671:             # Handler console
00672:             console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
00673:             console_formatter = logging.Formatter(
00674:                 '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00675:             )
00676:             console_handler.setFormatter(console_formatter)
00677:             logger.addHandler(console_handler)
00678:             
00679:             # Handler fichier
00680:             log_file = self.project_root / "logs" / "orchestrator.log"
00681:             log_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00682:             
00683:             file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8')
00684:             file_formatter = logging.Formatter(
00685:                 '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00686:             )
00687:             file_handler.setFormatter(file_formatter)
00688:             logger.addHandler(file_handler)
00689:         
00690:         return logger
00691:     
00692:     def _load_versions(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00693:         """Charge les versions des outils"""
00694:         versions_file = self.project_root / "config" / "versions.json"
00695:         if versions_file.exists():
00696:             with open(versions_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00697:                 return json.load(f)
00698:         return {}
00699:     
00700:     async def register_agent(self, agent_name: str, agent_instance):
00701:         """Enregistre un agent"""
00702:         self.agents[agent_name] = agent_instance
00703:         self.agent_status[agent_name] = {
00704:             "registered": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00705:             "status": "idle",
00706:             "tasks_completed": 0,
00707:             "last_active": None
00708:         }
00709:         
00710:         self.logger.info(f"Agent enregistré: {agent_name}")
00711:         
00712:         # Initialiser l'agent
00713:         try:
00714:             await agent_instance.initialize()
00715:             self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "ready"
00716:             self.logger.info(f"Agent {agent_name} initialisé avec succès")
00717:         except Exception as e:
00718:             self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00719:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de l'initialisation de {agent_name}: {e}")
00720:     
00721:     async def get_all_agents_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00722:         """Retourne les informations de tous les agents"""
00723:         agents_info = {}
00724:         for agent_name, agent_instance in self.agents.items():
00725:             try:
00726:                 agents_info[agent_name] = agent_instance.get_agent_info()
00727:                 agents_info[agent_name]["status"] = self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"]
00728:             except Exception as e:
00729:                 self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la récupération des infos de {agent_name}: {e}")
00730:         
00731:         return {
00732:             "total_agents": len(self.agents),
00733:             "agents": agents_info,
00734:             "system_versions": self.versions,
00735:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
00736:         }
00737:     
00738:     async def run_task_pipeline(self, pipeline_config: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00739:         """Exécute un pipeline de tâches"""
00740:         self.logger.info(f"Démarrage du pipeline: {pipeline_config.get('name', 'unnamed')}")
00741:         
00742:         results = {}
00743:         tasks = pipeline_config.get("tasks", [])
00744:         
00745:         for task in tasks:
00746:             task_name = task.get("name", "unnamed_task")
00747:             agent_name = task.get("agent")
00748:             
00749:             if agent_name not in self.agents:
00750:                 self.logger.error(f"Agent {agent_name} non trouvé pour la tâche {task_name}")
00751:                 continue
00752:             
00753:             self.logger.info(f"Exécution de la tâche {task_name} avec l'agent {agent_name}")
00754:             
00755:             try:
00756:                 # Mettre à jour le statut de l'agent
00757:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "busy"
00758:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["last_active"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
00759:                 
00760:                 # Exécuter la tâche
00761:                 result = await self.agents[agent_name].execute(
00762:                     task=task,
00763:                     context={
00764:                         "pipeline": pipeline_config,
00765:                         "previous_results": results,
00766:                         "versions": self.versions
00767:                     }
00768:                 )
00769:                 
00770:                 # Enregistrer le résultat
00771:                 results[task_name] = result
00772:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["tasks_completed"] += 1
00773:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "ready"
00774:                 
00775:                 self.logger.info(f"Tâche {task_name} terminée avec succès")
00776:                 
00777:             except asyncio.TimeoutError:
00778:                 self.logger.error(f"Timeout sur la tâche {task_name}")
00779:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "timeout"
00780:                 results[task_name] = {"status": "timeout", "error": "Task timeout"}
00781:                 
00782:             except Exception as e:
00783:                 self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de l'exécution de {task_name}: {e}")
00784:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00785:                 results[task_name] = {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
00786:         
00787:         # Sauvegarder les résultats
00788:         await self._save_pipeline_results(pipeline_config, results)
00789:         
00790:         return {
00791:             "pipeline": pipeline_config.get("name"),
00792:             "results": results,
00793:             "summary": self._generate_summary(results),
00794:             "agents_status": self.agent_status,
00795:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
00796:         }
00797:     
00798:     async def _save_pipeline_results(self, pipeline_config: Dict[str, Any], results: Dict[str, Any]):
00799:         """Sauvegarde les résultats du pipeline"""
00800:         try:
00801:             results_dir = self.project_root / "results" / "pipelines"
00802:             results_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00803:             
00804:             timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
00805:             pipeline_name = pipeline_config.get("name", "unnamed").replace(" ", "_").lower()
00806:             
00807:             result_file = results_dir / f"{pipeline_name}_{timestamp}.json"
00808:             
00809:             full_results = {
00810:                 "pipeline": pipeline_config,
00811:                 "results": results,
00812:                 "agents_info": await self.get_all_agents_info(),
00813:                 "system_versions": self.versions,
00814:                 "metadata": {
00815:                     "execution_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00816:                     "total_tasks": len(pipeline_config.get("tasks", [])),
00817:                     "successful_tasks": sum(1 for r in results.values() if r.get("status") == "success")
00818:                 }
00819:             }
00820:             
00821:             with open(result_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00822:                 json.dump(full_results, f, indent=2, default=str)
00823:             
00824:             self.logger.info(f"Résultats sauvegardés dans {result_file}")
00825:             
00826:         except Exception as e:
00827:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la sauvegarde des résultats: {e}")
00828:     
00829:     def _generate_summary(self, results: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00830:         """Génère un résumé des résultats"""
00831:         total = len(results)
00832:         successful = sum(1 for r in results.values() if r.get("status") in ["success", "completed"])
00833:         failed = total - successful
00834:         
00835:         return {
00836:             "total_tasks": total,
00837:             "successful_tasks": successful,
00838:             "failed_tasks": failed,
00839:             "success_rate": (successful / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
00840:         }
00841:     
00842:     async def health_check_all(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00843:         """Vérifie la santé de tous les agents"""
00844:         health_results = {}
00845:         
00846:         for agent_name, agent_instance in self.agents.items():
00847:             try:
00848:                 health = await agent_instance.health_check()
00849:                 health_results[agent_name] = health
00850:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["last_health_check"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
00851:             except Exception as e:
00852:                 health_results[agent_name] = {
00853:                     "status": "unhealthy",
00854:                     "error": str(e)
00855:                 }
00856:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00857:         
00858:         return {
00859:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00860:             "total_agents": len(self.agents),
00861:             "healthy_agents": sum(1 for h in health_results.values() if h.get("status") == "healthy"),
00862:             "agents": health_results
00863:         }
00864: '@

00525: 
00526: # 4. Créer le base_agent.py (classe parente)
00527: Write-Host "`n4. CREATION DE LA CLASSE BASE AGENT..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00528: $baseAgentCode = @'
00529: # agents/shared/base_agent.py
00530: import asyncio
00531: import json
00532: import logging
00533: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
00534: from pathlib import Path
00535: from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
00536: import yaml
00537: 
00538: class BaseAgent(ABC):
00539:     """Classe de base pour tous les agents"""
00540:     
00541:     def __init__(self, config_path: str):
00542:         self.config = self._load_config(config_path)
00543:         self.agent_id = self.config.get("agent_id", "unknown")
00544:         self.name = self.config.get("name", "Unnamed Agent")
00545:         self.version = self.config.get("version", "1.0.0")
00546:         self.logger = self._setup_logger()
00547:         self.memory = {}
00548:         self.context = {}
00549:         
00550:     def _load_config(self, config_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00551:         """Charge la configuration YAML"""
00552:         try:
00553:             with open(config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00554:                 return yaml.safe_load(f)
00555:         except Exception as e:
00556:             print(f"Erreur lors du chargement de la configuration: {e}")
00557:             return {}
00558:     
00559:     def _setup_logger(self) -> logging.Logger:
00560:         """Configure le logger"""
00561:         logger = logging.getLogger(self.agent_id)
00562:         if not logger.handlers:
00563:             logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
00564:             handler = logging.StreamHandler()
00565:             formatter = logging.Formatter(
00566:                 f'%(asctime)s - {self.agent_id} - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00567:             )
00568:             handler.setFormatter(formatter)
00569:             logger.addHandler(handler)
00570:         return logger
00571:     
00572:     @abstractmethod
00573:     async def initialize(self) -> bool:
00574:         """Initialise l'agent"""
00575:         pass
00576:     
00577:     @abstractmethod
00578:     async def execute(self, task: Dict[str, Any], context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00579:         """Exécute une tâche"""
00580:         pass
00581:     
00582:     async def load_context(self, context_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00583:         """Charge le contexte depuis un fichier"""
00584:         try:
00585:             if Path(context_path).exists():
00586:                 with open(context_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00587:                     self.context = json.load(f)
00588:                     self.logger.info(f"Contexte chargé depuis {context_path}")
00589:                     return self.context
00590:         except Exception as e:
00591:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors du chargement du contexte: {e}")
00592:         return {}
00593:     
00594:     async def save_memory(self, memory_path: str) -> bool:
00595:         """Sauvegarde la mémoire de l'agent"""
00596:         try:
00597:             memory_dir = Path(memory_path).parent
00598:             memory_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00599:             
00600:             with open(memory_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00601:                 json.dump(self.memory, f, indent=2)
00602:             
00603:             self.logger.info(f"Mémoire sauvegardée dans {memory_path}")
00604:             return True
00605:         except Exception as e:
00606:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la sauvegarde de la mémoire: {e}")
00607:             return False
00608:     
00609:     def get_agent_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00610:         """Retourne les informations de l'agent"""
00611:         return {
00612:             "agent_id": self.agent_id,
00613:             "name": self.name,
00614:             "version": self.version,
00615:             "config": self.config,
00616:             "tools": self.config.get("tools", []),
00617:             "dependencies": self.config.get("dependencies", {})
00618:         }
00619:     
00620:     async def health_check(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00621:         """Vérifie la santé de l'agent"""
00622:         return {
00623:             "status": "healthy",
00624:             "agent_id": self.agent_id,
00625:             "timestamp": asyncio.get_event_loop().time(),
00626:             "memory_usage": len(str(self.memory)),
00627:             "context_loaded": bool(self.context)
00628:         }
00629: '@
00630: 
00631: $baseAgentCode | Out-File -FilePath "$projectPath\agents\shared\base_agent.py" -Force -Encoding UTF8
00632: 
00633: # 5. Créer l'orchestrateur principal
00634: Write-Host "`n5. CREATION DE L'ORCHESTRATEUR PRINCIPAL..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00635: $orchestratorCode = @'
00636: # agents/orchestrator/orchestrator.py
00637: import asyncio
00638: import json
00639: import yaml
00640: from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional
00641: from pathlib import Path
00642: import logging
00643: from datetime import datetime
00644: 
00645: class Orchestrator:
00646:     """Orchestrateur principal qui gère tous les agents"""
00647:     
00648:     def __init__(self, project_root: str = "."):
00649:         self.project_root = Path(project_root)
00650:         self.agents = {}
00651:         self.agent_status = {}
00652:         self.task_queue = asyncio.Queue()
00653:         self.results = {}
00654:         self.versions = self._load_versions()
00655:         
00656:         # Configuration
00657:         self.config = {
00658:             "max_concurrent_tasks": 3,
00659:             "task_timeout": 300,  # 5 minutes
00660:             "retry_attempts": 3
00661:         }
00662:         
00663:         self.logger = self._setup_logger()
00664:     
00665:     def _setup_logger(self) -> logging.Logger:
00666:         """Configure le logger"""
00667:         logger = logging.getLogger("orchestrator")
00668:         logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
00669:         
00670:         if not logger.handlers:
00671:             # Handler console
00672:             console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
00673:             console_formatter = logging.Formatter(
00674:                 '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00675:             )
00676:             console_handler.setFormatter(console_formatter)
00677:             logger.addHandler(console_handler)
00678:             
00679:             # Handler fichier
00680:             log_file = self.project_root / "logs" / "orchestrator.log"
00681:             log_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00682:             
00683:             file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8')
00684:             file_formatter = logging.Formatter(
00685:                 '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
00686:             )
00687:             file_handler.setFormatter(file_formatter)
00688:             logger.addHandler(file_handler)
00689:         
00690:         return logger
00691:     
00692:     def _load_versions(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00693:         """Charge les versions des outils"""
00694:         versions_file = self.project_root / "config" / "versions.json"
00695:         if versions_file.exists():
00696:             with open(versions_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00697:                 return json.load(f)
00698:         return {}
00699:     
00700:     async def register_agent(self, agent_name: str, agent_instance):
00701:         """Enregistre un agent"""
00702:         self.agents[agent_name] = agent_instance
00703:         self.agent_status[agent_name] = {
00704:             "registered": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00705:             "status": "idle",
00706:             "tasks_completed": 0,
00707:             "last_active": None
00708:         }
00709:         
00710:         self.logger.info(f"Agent enregistré: {agent_name}")
00711:         
00712:         # Initialiser l'agent
00713:         try:
00714:             await agent_instance.initialize()
00715:             self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "ready"
00716:             self.logger.info(f"Agent {agent_name} initialisé avec succès")
00717:         except Exception as e:
00718:             self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00719:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de l'initialisation de {agent_name}: {e}")
00720:     
00721:     async def get_all_agents_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00722:         """Retourne les informations de tous les agents"""
00723:         agents_info = {}
00724:         for agent_name, agent_instance in self.agents.items():
00725:             try:
00726:                 agents_info[agent_name] = agent_instance.get_agent_info()
00727:                 agents_info[agent_name]["status"] = self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"]
00728:             except Exception as e:
00729:                 self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la récupération des infos de {agent_name}: {e}")
00730:         
00731:         return {
00732:             "total_agents": len(self.agents),
00733:             "agents": agents_info,
00734:             "system_versions": self.versions,
00735:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
00736:         }
00737:     
00738:     async def run_task_pipeline(self, pipeline_config: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00739:         """Exécute un pipeline de tâches"""
00740:         self.logger.info(f"Démarrage du pipeline: {pipeline_config.get('name', 'unnamed')}")
00741:         
00742:         results = {}
00743:         tasks = pipeline_config.get("tasks", [])
00744:         
00745:         for task in tasks:
00746:             task_name = task.get("name", "unnamed_task")
00747:             agent_name = task.get("agent")
00748:             
00749:             if agent_name not in self.agents:
00750:                 self.logger.error(f"Agent {agent_name} non trouvé pour la tâche {task_name}")
00751:                 continue
00752:             
00753:             self.logger.info(f"Exécution de la tâche {task_name} avec l'agent {agent_name}")
00754:             
00755:             try:
00756:                 # Mettre à jour le statut de l'agent
00757:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "busy"
00758:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["last_active"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
00759:                 
00760:                 # Exécuter la tâche
00761:                 result = await self.agents[agent_name].execute(
00762:                     task=task,
00763:                     context={
00764:                         "pipeline": pipeline_config,
00765:                         "previous_results": results,
00766:                         "versions": self.versions
00767:                     }
00768:                 )
00769:                 
00770:                 # Enregistrer le résultat
00771:                 results[task_name] = result
00772:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["tasks_completed"] += 1
00773:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "ready"
00774:                 
00775:                 self.logger.info(f"Tâche {task_name} terminée avec succès")
00776:                 
00777:             except asyncio.TimeoutError:
00778:                 self.logger.error(f"Timeout sur la tâche {task_name}")
00779:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "timeout"
00780:                 results[task_name] = {"status": "timeout", "error": "Task timeout"}
00781:                 
00782:             except Exception as e:
00783:                 self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de l'exécution de {task_name}: {e}")
00784:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00785:                 results[task_name] = {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
00786:         
00787:         # Sauvegarder les résultats
00788:         await self._save_pipeline_results(pipeline_config, results)
00789:         
00790:         return {
00791:             "pipeline": pipeline_config.get("name"),
00792:             "results": results,
00793:             "summary": self._generate_summary(results),
00794:             "agents_status": self.agent_status,
00795:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
00796:         }
00797:     
00798:     async def _save_pipeline_results(self, pipeline_config: Dict[str, Any], results: Dict[str, Any]):
00799:         """Sauvegarde les résultats du pipeline"""
00800:         try:
00801:             results_dir = self.project_root / "results" / "pipelines"
00802:             results_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
00803:             
00804:             timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
00805:             pipeline_name = pipeline_config.get("name", "unnamed").replace(" ", "_").lower()
00806:             
00807:             result_file = results_dir / f"{pipeline_name}_{timestamp}.json"
00808:             
00809:             full_results = {
00810:                 "pipeline": pipeline_config,
00811:                 "results": results,
00812:                 "agents_info": await self.get_all_agents_info(),
00813:                 "system_versions": self.versions,
00814:                 "metadata": {
00815:                     "execution_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00816:                     "total_tasks": len(pipeline_config.get("tasks", [])),
00817:                     "successful_tasks": sum(1 for r in results.values() if r.get("status") == "success")
00818:                 }
00819:             }
00820:             
00821:             with open(result_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
00822:                 json.dump(full_results, f, indent=2, default=str)
00823:             
00824:             self.logger.info(f"Résultats sauvegardés dans {result_file}")
00825:             
00826:         except Exception as e:
00827:             self.logger.error(f"Erreur lors de la sauvegarde des résultats: {e}")
00828:     
00829:     def _generate_summary(self, results: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00830:         """Génère un résumé des résultats"""
00831:         total = len(results)
00832:         successful = sum(1 for r in results.values() if r.get("status") in ["success", "completed"])
00833:         failed = total - successful
00834:         
00835:         return {
00836:             "total_tasks": total,
00837:             "successful_tasks": successful,
00838:             "failed_tasks": failed,
00839:             "success_rate": (successful / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
00840:         }
00841:     
00842:     async def health_check_all(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
00843:         """Vérifie la santé de tous les agents"""
00844:         health_results = {}
00845:         
00846:         for agent_name, agent_instance in self.agents.items():
00847:             try:
00848:                 health = await agent_instance.health_check()
00849:                 health_results[agent_name] = health
00850:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["last_health_check"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
00851:             except Exception as e:
00852:                 health_results[agent_name] = {
00853:                     "status": "unhealthy",
00854:                     "error": str(e)
00855:                 }
00856:                 self.agent_status[agent_name]["status"] = "error"
00857:         
00858:         return {
00859:             "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
00860:             "total_agents": len(self.agents),
00861:             "healthy_agents": sum(1 for h in health_results.values() if h.get("status") == "healthy"),
00862:             "agents": health_results
00863:         }

00041: # Fonction pour créer un Gist GitHub
00042: function New-GitHubGist {
00043:     param(
00044:         [string]$Token,
00045:         [string]$FileName,
00046:         [string]$Content,
00047:         [string]$Description
00048:     )
00049:     
00050:     try {
00051:         $Token = $Token.Trim()
00052:         
00053:         if ($Token -eq "ghp_********" -or $Token -eq "ghp_*" -or [string]::IsNullOrWhiteSpace($Token) -or $Token -match "^\*+$") {
00054:             return @{
00055:                 success = $false
00056:                 error = "Token invalide ou non configuré"
00057:             }
00058:         }
00059:         
00060:         $body = @{
00061:             description = $Description
00062:             public = $false
00063:             files = @{
00064:                 $FileName = @{content = $Content}
00065:             }
00066:         }
00067:         
00068:         $jsonBody = $body | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 10
00069:         
00070:         $headers = @{
00071:             Authorization = "token $Token"
00072:             Accept = "application/vnd.github.v3+json"
00073:             "User-Agent" = "PowerShell-Gist-Uploader"
00074:         }
00075:         
00076:         $response = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "https://api.github.com/gists" `
00077:                                      -Method POST `
00078:                                      -Headers $headers `
00079:                                      -Body $jsonBody `
00080:                                      -ContentType "application/json" `
00081:                                      -ErrorAction Stop
00082:         
00083:         return @{
00084:             success = $true
00085:             url = $response.html_url
00086:             id = $response.id
00087:         }
00088:     } catch {
00089:         $errorMsg = $_.Exception.Message
00090:         
00091:         if ($errorMsg -like "*401*") {
00092:             $errorMsg = "Token GitHub invalide ou expiré (401). Regénérez un token avec permission 'gist'."
00093:         } elseif ($errorMsg -like "*403*") {
00094:             $errorMsg = "Accès refusé (403). Vérifiez les permissions du token."
00095:         }
00096:         
00097:         return @{
00098:             success = $false
00099:             error = $errorMsg
00100:         }
00101:     }
00102: }
00103: 
00104: # Fonction pour tester le token GitHub
00105: function Test-GitHubToken {
00106:     param([string]$Token)
00107:     
00108:     try {
00109:         $headers = @{
00110:             Authorization = "token $Token"
00111:             Accept = "application/vnd.github.v3+json"
00112:             "User-Agent" = "PowerShell-Test"
00113:         }
00114:         
00115:         $response = Invoke-WebRequest -Uri "https://api.github.com/user" -Headers $headers -ErrorAction Stop
00116:         $user = $response.Content | ConvertFrom-Json
00117:         
00118:         return @{
00119:             valid = $true
00120:             username = $user.login
00121:         }
00122:     } catch {
00123:         $errorMsg = $_.Exception.Message
00124:         if ($errorMsg -like "*401*") {
00125:             $errorMsg = "Token invalide ou expiré (401 Unauthorized)"
00126:         }
00127:         
00128:         return @{
00129:             valid = $false
00130:             error = $errorMsg
00131:         }
00132:     }
00133: }
00134: 
00135: # Fonction pour publier sur GitHub Repository - SANS INTERACTION
00136: # Fonction CORRIGÉE pour publier sur GitHub Repository - PROBLÈME DE RÉPERTOIRE FIXÉ
00137: function Publish-ToGitHubRepo {
00138:     param(
00139:         [string]$Token,
00140:         [string]$Username,
00141:         [string]$RepoName,
00142:         [string]$Description,
00143:         [bool]$IsPrivate
00144:     )
00145:     
00146:     Write-Host "`n=== PUBLICATION SUR GITHUB REPOSITORY ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00147:     
00148:     # Vérifier et nettoyer le token
00149:     $Token = $Token.Trim()
00150:     
00151:     # Log pour débogage
00152:     Write-Host "Token (premiers 10 chars): $($Token.Substring(0, [math]::Min(10, $Token.Length)))..." -ForegroundColor Gray
00153:     Write-Host "Longueur token: $($Token.Length)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00154:     
00155:     if ($Token -match "^\*+$" -or $Token -eq "ghp_********" -or [string]::IsNullOrWhiteSpace($Token)) {
00156:         Write-Host "❌ Token vide ou masqué" -ForegroundColor Red
00157:         return @{ success = $false; error = "Token GitHub vide ou masqué" }
00158:     }
00159:     
00160:     if (-not $Token.StartsWith("ghp_")) {
00161:         Write-Host "❌ Format de token invalide (doit commencer par 'ghp_')" -ForegroundColor Red
00162:         return @{ success = $false; error = "Format de token invalide" }
00163:     }
00164:     
00165:     try {
00166:         # Vérifier si Git est installé
00167:         try {
00168:             git --version | Out-Null
00169:         } catch {
00170:             Write-Host "✗ Git non trouvé sur le système" -ForegroundColor Red
00171:             Write-Host "Installation requise: https://git-scm.com/downloads" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00172:             return @{ success = $false; error = "Git non installé" }
00173:         }
00174:         
00175:         # Vérifier si le dossier existe
00176:         if (-not (Test-Path $PROJECT_PATH)) {
00177:             Write-Host "Création du dossier: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00178:             New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $PROJECT_PATH -Force | Out-Null
00179:         }
00180:         
00181:         # Sauvegarder le répertoire de travail actuel
00182:         $originalLocation = Get-Location
00183:         
00184:         # CRITIQUE: Se déplacer dans le dossier du projet AVANT toute opération Git
00185:         Write-Host "Changement vers le dossier du projet: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00186:         Set-Location -Path $PROJECT_PATH -ErrorAction Stop
00187:         
00188:         # Vérifier où nous sommes maintenant
00189:         $currentDir = Get-Location
00190:         Write-Host "Répertoire actuel: $currentDir" -ForegroundColor Gray
00191:         
00192:         # Nettoyer toute configuration Git problématique
00193:         Write-Host "Nettoyage configuration Git..." -NoNewline
00194:         git config --global --unset credential.helper 2>$null
00195:         git config --global credential.helper "" 2>$null
00196:         git config --global --unset credential.modalprompt 2>$null
00197:         
00198:         # Ajouter le répertoire courant à safe.directory
00199:         git config --global --add safe.directory $currentDir.Path 2>$null
00200:         Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00201:         
00202:         # Initialiser Git si pas déjà fait
00203:         if (-not (Test-Path ".git")) {
00204:             Write-Host "Initialisation du dépôt Git..." -NoNewline
00205:             git init | Out-Null
00206:             Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00207:         } else {
00208:             Write-Host "✓ Dépôt Git déjà initialisé" -ForegroundColor Gray
00209:         }
00210:         
00211:         # Créer le .gitignore
00212:         $gitignoreContent = @"
00213: # Fichiers générés par le script
00214: PROJECT_SHARE_*
00215: GISTS_INDEX*
00216: GITHUB_PUBLISH_*
00217: "@
00218:         $gitignoreContent | Out-File -FilePath ".gitignore" -Encoding UTF8 -Force
00219:         
00220:         # Configurer Git
00221:         Write-Host "Configuration Git..." -NoNewline
00222:         
00223:         # IMPORTANT: Configurer l'URL avec le token - Méthode plus robuste
00224:         $encodedToken = [System.Web.HttpUtility]::UrlEncode($Token)
00225:         $remoteUrl = "https://${Username}:${encodedToken}@github.com/${Username}/${RepoName}.git"
00226:         
00227:         Write-Host " URL: https://${Username}:***@github.com/${Username}/${RepoName}.git" -ForegroundColor Gray
00228:         
00229:         # Supprimer tout remote existant
00230:         git remote remove origin 2>$null
00231:         
00232:         # Ajouter le nouveau remote
00233:         git remote add origin $remoteUrl
00234:         
00235:         # Configurer le nom et email
00236:         git config user.name "$Username"
00237:         git config user.email "$Username@users.noreply.github.com"
00238:         
00239:         # Désactiver les prompts Git
00240:         git config --global credential.helper store
00241:         git config --global credential.modalprompt false
00242:         
00243:         Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00244:         
00245:         # Ajouter tous les fichiers (sauf ceux exclus)
00246:         Write-Host "Ajout des fichiers..." -NoNewline
00247:         
00248:         # Créer un fichier .gitignore temporaire pour exclure les fichiers générés
00249:         $tempGitignore = @"
00250: # Fichiers générés par le script
00251: PROJECT_SHARE_*
00252: GISTS_INDEX*
00253: GITHUB_PUBLISH_*
00254: *.bak
00255: *.tmp
00256: "@
00257:         $tempGitignore | Out-File -FilePath ".gitignore" -Encoding UTF8 -Force
00258:         
00259:         # Ajouter tous les fichiers
00260:         git add . 2>&1 | Out-Null
00261:         Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00262:         
00263:         # Faire le commit
00264:         $commitMessage = "🚀 Publication automatique: $PROJECT_NAME - $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')"
00265:         Write-Host "Commit..." -NoNewline
00266:         git commit -m $commitMessage --quiet 2>&1 | Out-Null
00267:         Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00268:         
00269:         # Pousser sur GitHub
00270:         Write-Host "Push vers GitHub..." -NoNewline
00271:         
00272:         # Forcer la branche main
00273:         git branch -M main --quiet 2>&1 | Out-Null
00274:         
00275:         # Variables d'environnement pour désactiver les prompts
00276:         $env:GIT_TERMINAL_PROMPT = "0"
00277:         $env:GCM_INTERACTIVE = "Never"
00278:         
00279:         # Exécuter le push
00280:         $pushOutput = git push -u origin main --force 2>&1
00281:         
00282:         if ($LASTEXITCODE -eq 0) {
00283:             Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00284:             Write-Host "✅ Publication réussie!" -ForegroundColor Green
00285:             
00286:             # Vérifier le dernier commit
00287:             $lastCommit = git log --oneline -1
00288:             
00289:             # Retourner au répertoire original
00290:             Set-Location -Path $originalLocation
00291:             
00292:             return @{
00293:                 success = $true
00294:                 repo_url = "https://github.com/$Username/$RepoName"
00295:                 commit = $lastCommit
00296:                 message = "Publication réussie"
00297:             }
00298:         } else {
00299:             Write-Host " ✗" -ForegroundColor Red
00300:             
00301:             # Analyser l'erreur
00302:             $errorMsg = "Erreur Git inconnue"
00303:             
00304:             if ($pushOutput -match "Authentication failed" -or $pushOutput -match "invalid credentials") {
00305:                 $errorMsg = "Authentification échouée - Token GitHub invalide ou expiré"
00306:                 Write-Host "❌ Token invalide - Regénérez-le sur: https://github.com/settings/tokens" -ForegroundColor Red
00307:             } elseif ($pushOutput -match "remote: Repository not found") {
00308:                 $errorMsg = "Le repository n'existe pas. Créez-le d'abord sur GitHub."
00309:                 Write-Host "❌ Repository non trouvé - Créez-le sur GitHub d'abord" -ForegroundColor Red
00310:             } elseif ($pushOutput -match "remote: Permission to") {
00311:                 $errorMsg = "Permission refusée - Vérifiez que le token a les droits 'repo'"
00312:                 Write-Host "❌ Permission refusée - Le token doit avoir la permission 'repo'" -ForegroundColor Red
00313:             } else {
00314:                 $errorMsg = "Erreur Git: $($pushOutput.Trim())"
00315:                 Write-Host "❌ Erreur: $($pushOutput.Trim())" -ForegroundColor Red
00316:             }
00317:             
00318:             # Afficher des conseils de dépannage
00319:             Write-Host "`n=== CONSEILS DE DÉPANNAGE ===" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00320:             Write-Host "Répertoire actuel: $(Get-Location)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00321:             Write-Host "Répertoire projet: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Gray
00322:             
00323:             # Retourner au répertoire original
00324:             Set-Location -Path $originalLocation
00325:             
00326:             return @{
00327:                 success = $false
00328:                 error = $errorMsg
00329:                 git_output = $pushOutput.Trim()
00330:                 current_directory = $currentDir.Path
00331:             }
00332:         }
00333:         
00334:     } catch {
00335:         Write-Host " ✗" -ForegroundColor Red
00336:         Write-Host "❌ Erreur inattendue: $_" -ForegroundColor Red
00337:         
00338:         # Essayer de retourner au répertoire original
00339:         try {
00340:             Set-Location -Path $originalLocation -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
00341:         } catch {
00342:             # Ignorer si on ne peut pas revenir
00343:         }
00344:         
00345:         return @{
00346:             success = $false
00347:             error = $_.Exception.Message
00348:         }
00349:     }
00350: }
00351: 
00352: # Fonction pour générer des fichiers locaux
00353: function Generate-LocalFiles {
00354:     Write-Host "`n=== GÉNÉRATION DE FICHIERS LOCAUX ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00355:     
00356:     # Analyser tous les fichiers du projet
00357:     Write-Host "Analyse des fichiers dans: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00358:     
00359:     $allFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path $PROJECT_PATH -Recurse -File | Where-Object {
00360:         $relativePath = $_.FullName.Replace($PROJECT_PATH, "").TrimStart('\')
00361:         -not (Should-ExcludePath -Path $relativePath)
00362:     }
00363:     
00364:     Write-Host "Nombre de fichiers trouvés: $($allFiles.Count)" -ForegroundColor Green
00365:     
00366:     if ($allFiles.Count -eq 0) {
00367:         Write-Host "Aucun fichier à traiter." -ForegroundColor Yellow
00368:         return @{ success = $false; error = "Aucun fichier trouvé" }
00369:     }
00370:     
00371:     # Créer un fichier d'index
00372:     $indexContent = @"
00373: INDEX DES FICHIERS DU PROJET: $PROJECT_NAME
00374: Date de génération: $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')
00375: Chemin du projet: $PROJECT_PATH
00376: 
00377: LISTE DES FICHIERS:
00378: "@
00379:     
00380:     $fileIndex = 1
00381:     $processedFiles = @()
00382:     
00383:     foreach ($file in $allFiles) {
00384:         $relativePath = $file.FullName.Replace($PROJECT_PATH, "").TrimStart('\')
00385:         $fileSizeKB = [math]::Round($file.Length / 1KB, 2)
00386:         
00387:         $indexContent += "`n$fileIndex. $relativePath (${fileSizeKB} KB)"
00388:         $fileIndex++
00389:         
00390:         $processedFiles += @{
00391:             FullPath = $file.FullName
00392:             RelativePath = $relativePath
00393:             Size = $file.Length
00394:             ProcessedSize = $file.Length
00395:         }
00396:     }
00397:     
00398:     # Écrire le fichier d'index
00399:     $indexContent | Out-File -FilePath $INDEX_FILENAME -Encoding UTF8
00400:     Write-Host "✅ Fichier d'index créé: $INDEX_FILENAME" -ForegroundColor Green
00401:     
00402:     # Générer des fichiers partagés si nécessaire
00403:     $totalSize = ($processedFiles | Measure-Object -Property Size -Sum).Sum
00404:     $totalSizeMB = [math]::Round($totalSize / 1MB, 2)
00405:     
00406:     Write-Host "Taille totale des fichiers: ${totalSizeMB} MB" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00407:     
00408:     if ($totalSize -gt $MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
00409:         Write-Host "Le projet est trop volumineux, génération de fichiers partagés..." -ForegroundColor Cyan
00410:         
00411:         $groups = Optimize-FileGrouping -Files $processedFiles -MaxSize $MAX_FILE_SIZE -TargetSize $TARGET_FILE_SIZE
00412:         
00413:         $shareFiles = @()
00414:         $groupIndex = 1
00415:         
00416:         foreach ($group in $groups) {
00417:             $shareFileName = "${SHARE_FILENAME_PREFIX}_PART${groupIndex}.txt"
00418:             $shareContent = @"
00419: FICHIER PARTAGÉ: $shareFileName
00420: Projet: $PROJECT_NAME
00421: Partie: $groupIndex/$($groups.Count)
00422: Date: $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')
00423: Taille totale: $([math]::Round($group.TotalSize/1KB, 2)) KB
00424: 
00425: "@
00426:             
00427:             foreach ($file in $group.Files) {
00428:                 $fileContent = Get-Content -Path $file.FullPath -Raw -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
00429:                 if ($fileContent) {
00430:                     $shareContent += "=" * 60 + "`n"
00431:                     $shareContent += "FICHIER: $($file.RelativePath)`n"
00432:                     $shareContent += "TAILLE: $([math]::Round($file.Size/1KB, 2)) KB`n"
00433:                     $shareContent += "=" * 60 + "`n`n"
00434:                     $shareContent += Add-LineNumbers -Content $fileContent
00435:                     $shareContent += "`n`n"
00436:                 }
00437:             }
00438:             
00439:             $shareContent | Out-File -FilePath $shareFileName -Encoding UTF8
00440:             $shareFiles += $shareFileName
00441:             Write-Host "  Fichier créé: $shareFileName ($([math]::Round($group.TotalSize/1KB, 2)) KB)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00442:             $groupIndex++
00443:         }
00444:         
00445:         Write-Host "✅ $($groups.Count) fichier(s) partagé(s) créé(s)" -ForegroundColor Green
00446:         
00447:         return @{
00448:             success = $true
00449:             index_file = $INDEX_FILENAME
00450:             share_files = $shareFiles
00451:             total_size = $totalSize
00452:             file_count = $allFiles.Count
00453:         }
00454:     } else {
00455:         Write-Host "Le projet tient dans un seul fichier." -ForegroundColor Green
00456:         return @{
00457:             success = $true
00458:             index_file = $INDEX_FILENAME
00459:             total_size = $totalSize
00460:             file_count = $allFiles.Count
00461:         }
00462:     }
00463: }

00465: # Fonction pour partager sur GitHub Gists
00466: function Share-ToGitHubGists {
00467:     Write-Host "`n=== PARTAGE SUR GITHUB GISTS ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00468:     
00469:     # Vérifier le token
00470:     if (-not $GITHUB_TOKEN -or $GITHUB_TOKEN -match "^\*+$" -or $GITHUB_TOKEN -eq "ghp_********") {
00471:         Write-Host "❌ Token GitHub non configuré" -ForegroundColor Red
00472:         return @{ success = $false; error = "Token GitHub manquant" }
00473:     }
00474:     
00475:     # Générer d'abord les fichiers locaux
00476:     $localResult = Generate-LocalFiles
00477:     if (-not $localResult.success) {
00478:         return $localResult
00479:     }
00480:     
00481:     $gists = @()
00482:     
00483:     # Partager le fichier d'index
00484:     if (Test-Path $INDEX_FILENAME) {
00485:         $indexContent = Get-Content -Path $INDEX_FILENAME -Raw
00486:         $indexGist = New-GitHubGist -Token $GITHUB_TOKEN `
00487:                                    -FileName "$($PROJECT_NAME)_INDEX.txt" `
00488:                                    -Content $indexContent `
00489:                                    -Description "Index du projet $PROJECT_NAME"
00490:         
00491:         if ($indexGist.success) {
00492:             Write-Host "✅ Index partagé: $($indexGist.url)" -ForegroundColor Green
00493:             $gists += @{
00494:                 type = "index"
00495:                 url = $indexGist.url
00496:             }
00497:         } else {
00498:             Write-Host "❌ Erreur partage index: $($indexGist.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00499:         }
00500:     }
00501:     
00502:     # Partager les fichiers de partage
00503:     if ($localResult.share_files) {
00504:         $fileIndexCounter = 1
00505:         foreach ($shareFile in $localResult.share_files) {
00506:             if (Test-Path $shareFile) {
00507:                 $fileContent = Get-Content -Path $shareFile -Raw
00508:                 $gistResult = New-GitHubGist -Token $GITHUB_TOKEN `
00509:                                             -FileName "$($PROJECT_NAME)_PART${fileIndexCounter}.txt" `
00510:                                             -Content $fileContent `
00511:                                             -Description "Partie $fileIndexCounter du projet $PROJECT_NAME"
00512:                 
00513:                 if ($gistResult.success) {
00514:                     Write-Host "✅ Partie $fileIndexCounter partagée: $($gistResult.url)" -ForegroundColor Green
00515:                     $gists += @{
00516:                         type = "part"
00517:                         part = $fileIndexCounter
00518:                         url = $gistResult.url
00519:                     }
00520:                 } else {
00521:                     Write-Host "❌ Erreur partie $fileIndexCounter : $($gistResult.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00522:                 }
00523:                 $fileIndexCounter++
00524:             }
00525:         }
00526:     }
00527:     
00528:     # Créer un index des Gists
00529:     if ($gists.Count -gt 0) {
00530:         $gistsIndex = @"
00531: INDEX DES GISTS GITHUB - $PROJECT_NAME
00532: Date: $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')
00533: 
00534: "@
00535:         
00536:         foreach ($gist in $gists) {
00537:             if ($gist.type -eq "index") {
00538:                 $gistsIndex += "📄 INDEX: $($gist.url)`n"
00539:             } else {
00540:                 $gistsIndex += "📦 PARTIE $($gist.part): $($gist.url)`n"
00541:             }
00542:         }
00543:         
00544:         $timestamp = Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss'
00545:         $gistsIndexFile = "GISTS_INDEX_${timestamp}.txt"
00546:         $gistsIndex | Out-File -FilePath $gistsIndexFile -Encoding UTF8
00547:         Write-Host "✅ Index des Gists créé localement: $gistsIndexFile" -ForegroundColor Green
00548:         
00549:         return @{
00550:             success = $true
00551:             gists = $gists
00552:             gists_count = $gists.Count
00553:             index_file = $gistsIndexFile
00554:         }
00555:     } else {
00556:         return @{
00557:             success = $false
00558:             error = "Aucun Gist n'a pu être créé"
00559:         }
00560:     }
00561: }
00562: 
00563: # Fonction pour l'optimisation
00564: function Optimize-FileGrouping {
00565:     param(
00566:         [array]$Files,
00567:         [int]$MaxSize,
00568:         [int]$TargetSize
00569:     )
00570:     
00571:     $sortedFiles = $Files | Sort-Object @{Expression = {$_.ProcessedSize}; Descending = $true}
00572:     
00573:     $groups = @()
00574:     $currentGroup = @()
00575:     $currentSize = 0
00576:     
00577:     foreach ($file in $sortedFiles) {
00578:         $fileSize = $file.ProcessedSize
00579:         
00580:         if ($fileSize -gt $MaxSize) {
00581:             Write-Host "  AVERTISSEMENT: $($file.RelativePath) est trop gros ($([math]::Round($fileSize/1KB, 2)) Ko) - sera dans son propre fichier" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00582:             if ($currentGroup.Count -gt 0) {
00583:                 $groups += @{
00584:                     Files = $currentGroup
00585:                     TotalSize = $currentSize
00586:                 }
00587:                 $currentGroup = @()
00588:                 $currentSize = 0
00589:             }
00590:             $groups += @{
00591:                 Files = @($file)
00592:                 TotalSize = $fileSize
00593:             }
00594:             continue
00595:         }
00596:         
00597:         if (($currentSize + $fileSize) -gt $TargetSize -and $currentGroup.Count -gt 0) {
00598:             $groups += @{
00599:                 Files = $currentGroup
00600:                 TotalSize = $currentSize
00601:             }
00602:             $currentGroup = @()
00603:             $currentSize = 0
00604:         }
00605:         
00606:         $currentGroup += $file
00607:         $currentSize += $fileSize
00608:     }
00609:     
00610:     if ($currentGroup.Count -gt 0) {
00611:         $groups += @{
00612:             Files = $currentGroup
00613:             TotalSize = $currentSize
00614:         }
00615:     }
00616:     
00617:     return $groups
00618: }
00619: 
00620: # Fonction pour ajouter des numéros de ligne
00621: function Add-LineNumbers {
00622:     param([string]$Content)
00623:     
00624:     if (-not $SHOW_LINE_NUMBERS) { return $Content }
00625:     
00626:     $lines = $Content -split "`n"
00627:     $result = @()
00628:     $i = 1
00629:     
00630:     foreach ($line in $lines) {
00631:         $result += "{0:D5}: {1}" -f $i, $line
00632:         $i++
00633:     }
00634:     
00635:     return $result -join "`n"
00636: }
00637: 
00638: # Fonction pour vérifier les exclusions
00639: function Should-ExcludePath {
00640:     param([string]$Path)
00641:     
00642:     if ($Path -like "*${SHARE_FILENAME_PREFIX}_*" -or $Path -like "*GISTS_INDEX*" -or $Path -like "*GITHUB_PUBLISH_*") {
00643:         return $true
00644:     }
00645:     
00646:     foreach ($pattern in $EXCLUDE_PATTERNS) {
00647:         if ($pattern -match "^\*\.") {
00648:             $ext = $pattern.Substring(1)
00649:             if ($Path -like "*$ext") { return $true }
00650:         }
00651:         elseif ($Path -like "*$pattern*") {
00652:             return $true
00653:         }
00654:     }
00655:     return $false
00656: }

00659: # SCRIPT PRINCIPAL
00660: # ============================================================================
00661: 
00662: Clear-Host
00663: Write-Host ""
00664: Write-Host ("=" * 60) -ForegroundColor Cyan
00665: Write-Host "SHARE SPLIT 1M - $PROJECT_NAME" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00666: Write-Host ("=" * 60) -ForegroundColor Cyan
00667: Write-Host ""
00668: 
00669: # Vérifier le dossier
00670: if (-not (Test-Path $PROJECT_PATH)) {
00671:     Write-Host "ERREUR: Chemin introuvable: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Red
00672:     exit 1
00673: }
00674: 
00675: Write-Host "Chemin: $PROJECT_PATH" -ForegroundColor Green
00676: Write-Host ""
00677: 
00678: # ============================================================================
00679: # CONNEXION AUTOMATIQUE À GITHUB (NON INTERACTIVE)
00680: # ============================================================================
00681: 
00682: $autoConnectSuccess = $false
00683: $showMenu = $true
00684: 
00685: # Correction du pattern regex pour éviter l'erreur
00686: $validTokenPattern = "ghp_[a-zA-Z0-9]{36,}"
00687: 
00688: # Vérifier si la configuration GitHub est complète
00689: if ($GITHUB_TOKEN -and $GITHUB_TOKEN -match $validTokenPattern -and 
00690:     $GITHUB_USERNAME -and $GITHUB_REPO_NAME -and
00691:     $GITHUB_TOKEN -notmatch "^\*+$" -and $GITHUB_TOKEN -ne "ghp_********") {
00692:     
00693:     Write-Host "=== CONNEXION AUTOMATIQUE GITHUB ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00694:     Write-Host "Configuration GitHub détectée" -ForegroundColor Green
00695:     Write-Host "Utilisateur: $GITHUB_USERNAME" -ForegroundColor Gray
00696:     Write-Host "Repository: $GITHUB_REPO_NAME" -ForegroundColor Gray
00697:     Write-Host ""
00698:     
00699:     # Tester le token d'abord
00700:     Write-Host "Vérification du token GitHub..." -NoNewline
00701:     $tokenTest = Test-GitHubToken -Token $GITHUB_TOKEN
00702:     
00703:     if ($tokenTest.valid) {
00704:         Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00705:         Write-Host "Token valide pour: $($tokenTest.username)" -ForegroundColor Green
00706:         
00707:         # Vérifier si le repository existe
00708:         Write-Host "Vérification du repository..." -NoNewline
00709:         $headers = @{
00710:             Authorization = "token $GITHUB_TOKEN"
00711:             Accept = "application/vnd.github.v3+json"
00712:         }
00713:         
00714:         try {
00715:             $repoCheck = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "https://api.github.com/repos/$GITHUB_USERNAME/$GITHUB_REPO_NAME" `
00716:                                           -Headers $headers `
00717:                                           -ErrorAction Stop
00718:             Write-Host " ✓ (existe déjà)" -ForegroundColor Green
00719:             $repoExists = $true
00720:         } catch {
00721:             # Le repository n'existe pas, le créer automatiquement
00722:             Write-Host " ✗ (n'existe pas)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00723:             Write-Host "Création automatique du repository..." -NoNewline
00724:             
00725:             $body = @{
00726:                 name = $GITHUB_REPO_NAME
00727:                 description = $GITHUB_REPO_DESCRIPTION
00728:                 private = $GITHUB_REPO_PRIVATE
00729:             } | ConvertTo-Json
00730:             
00731:             try {
00732:                 $newRepo = Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "https://api.github.com/user/repos" `
00733:                                              -Method POST `
00734:                                              -Headers $headers `
00735:                                              -Body $body `
00736:                                              -ContentType "application/json"
00737:                 Write-Host " ✓" -ForegroundColor Green
00738:                 $repoExists = $true
00739:             } catch {
00740:                 Write-Host " ✗" -ForegroundColor Red
00741:                 Write-Host "Erreur création: $_" -ForegroundColor Red
00742:                 $repoExists = $false
00743:             }
00744:         }
00745:         
00746:         if ($repoExists) {
00747:             # Publier sur GitHub automatiquement
00748:             Write-Host "Publication automatique sur GitHub..." -ForegroundColor Cyan
00749:             
00750:             $result = Publish-ToGitHubRepo -Token $GITHUB_TOKEN `
00751:                                           -Username $GITHUB_USERNAME `
00752:                                           -RepoName $GITHUB_REPO_NAME `
00753:                                           -Description $GITHUB_REPO_DESCRIPTION `
00754:                                           -IsPrivate $GITHUB_REPO_PRIVATE
00755:             
00756:             if ($result.success) {
00757:                 $autoConnectSuccess = $true
00758:                 Write-Host ""
00759:                 Write-Host "✅ CONNEXION AUTOMATIQUE RÉUSSIE !" -ForegroundColor Green
00760:                 Write-Host "Repository: $($result.repo_url)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00761:                 Write-Host "Commit: $($result.commit)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00762:                 Write-Host ""
00763:                 
00764:                 # Demander si on veut voir le menu
00765:                 $showMenuAnswer = Read-Host "Voulez-vous voir le menu principal ? (O/N)"
00766:                 if ($showMenuAnswer -eq 'O' -or $showMenuAnswer -eq 'o') {
00767:                     $showMenu = $true
00768:                 } else {
00769:                     Write-Host "Au revoir!" -ForegroundColor Green
00770:                     exit 0
00771:                 }
00772:             } else {
00773:                 Write-Host ""
00774:                 Write-Host "❌ Connexion automatique échouée" -ForegroundColor Red
00775:                 if ($result.error) {
00776:                     Write-Host "Erreur: $($result.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00777:                 }
00778:                 Write-Host ""
00779:                 $showMenu = $true
00780:             }
00781:         } else {
00782:             Write-Host "❌ Impossible de créer le repository" -ForegroundColor Red
00783:             $showMenu = $true
00784:         }
00785:     } else {
00786:         Write-Host " ✗" -ForegroundColor Red
00787:         Write-Host "❌ Token GitHub invalide" -ForegroundColor Red
00788:         Write-Host "Erreur: $($tokenTest.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00789:         Write-Host ""
00790:         $showMenu = $true
00791:     }
00792: } else {
00793:     Write-Host "⚠ Configuration GitHub incomplète ou token masqué" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00794:     Write-Host "   Impossible de se connecter automatiquement à GitHub" -ForegroundColor Gray
00795:     Write-Host ""
00796:     $showMenu = $true
00797: }
00798: 
00799: # ============================================================================
00800: # MENU PRINCIPAL
00801: # ============================================================================
00802: 
00803: if ($showMenu) {
00804:     do {
00805:         Clear-Host
00806:         Write-Host ""
00807:         Write-Host ("=" * 60) -ForegroundColor Cyan
00808:         Write-Host "SHARE SPLIT 1M - $PROJECT_NAME" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00809:         Write-Host ("=" * 60) -ForegroundColor Cyan
00810:         Write-Host ""
00811:         
00812:         if ($autoConnectSuccess) {
00813:             Write-Host "✅ Publication GitHub déjà effectuée" -ForegroundColor Green
00814:             Write-Host ""
00815:         }
00816:         
00817:         Write-Host "=== MENU PRINCIPAL ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00818:         Write-Host "1. Publier sur GitHub Repository" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00819:         Write-Host "2. Partager sur GitHub Gists" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00820:         Write-Host "3. Générer seulement les fichiers locaux" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00821:         Write-Host "4. Quitter" -ForegroundColor Red
00822:         Write-Host ""
00823:         
00824:         $choice = Read-Host "Votre choix [1-4]"
00825:         
00826:         switch ($choice) {
00827:             '1' {
00828:                 # OPTION 1: GitHub Repository
00829:                 Write-Host "`n=== PUBLICATION GITHUB REPOSITORY ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00830:                 
00831:                 # Demander les informations manquantes
00832:                 if (-not $GITHUB_TOKEN -or $GITHUB_TOKEN -match "^\*+$" -or $GITHUB_TOKEN -eq "ghp_********") {
00833:                     Write-Host ""
00834:                     Write-Host "🔑 TOKEN GITHUB REQUIS" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00835:                     Write-Host "Pour créer un token:" -ForegroundColor Gray
00836:                     Write-Host "1. https://github.com/settings/tokens" -ForegroundColor Gray
00837:                     Write-Host "2. 'Generate new token (classic)'" -ForegroundColor Gray
00838:                     Write-Host "3. Donnez un nom" -ForegroundColor Gray
00839:                     Write-Host "4. Sélectionnez 'repo' (TOUTE la section)" -ForegroundColor Green
00840:                     Write-Host "5. 'Generate token'" -ForegroundColor Gray
00841:                     Write-Host "6. Copiez le token (commence par 'ghp_')" -ForegroundColor Gray
00842:                     Write-Host ""
00843:                     
00844:                     $GITHUB_TOKEN = Read-Host "Collez votre token GitHub"
00845:                 }
00846:                 
00847:                 if (-not $GITHUB_USERNAME) {
00848:                     $GITHUB_USERNAME = Read-Host "Nom d'utilisateur GitHub"
00849:                 }
00850:                 
00851:                 if (-not $GITHUB_REPO_NAME) {
00852:                     $GITHUB_REPO_NAME = Read-Host "Nom du repository"
00853:                 }
00854:                 
00855:                 # Publier sur GitHub
00856:                 $result = Publish-ToGitHubRepo -Token $GITHUB_TOKEN `
00857:                                               -Username $GITHUB_USERNAME `
00858:                                               -RepoName $GITHUB_REPO_NAME `
00859:                                               -Description $GITHUB_REPO_DESCRIPTION `
00860:                                               -IsPrivate $GITHUB_REPO_PRIVATE
00861:                 
00862:                 if ($result.success) {
00863:                     Write-Host ""
00864:                     Write-Host "✅ Publication réussie sur GitHub!" -ForegroundColor Green
00865:                     Write-Host "Repository: $($result.repo_url)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00866:                     Write-Host "Commit: $($result.commit)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00867:                     $autoConnectSuccess = $true
00868:                 } else {
00869:                     Write-Host ""
00870:                     Write-Host "❌ Échec de la publication" -ForegroundColor Red
00871:                     Write-Host "Erreur: $($result.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00872:                 }
00873:                 
00874:                 Write-Host ""
00875:                 Write-Host "Appuyez sur Entrée pour continuer..."
00876:                 Read-Host
00877:             }
00878:             
00879:             '2' {
00880:                 # OPTION 2: GitHub Gists
00881:                 $result = Share-ToGitHubGists
00882:                 if ($result.success) {
00883:                     Write-Host ""
00884:                     Write-Host "✅ Partage Gists réussi!" -ForegroundColor Green
00885:                     Write-Host "Nombre de Gists créés: $($result.gists_count)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00886:                     Write-Host "Index local créé: $($result.index_file)" -ForegroundColor Gray
00887:                 } else {
00888:                     Write-Host ""
00889:                     Write-Host "❌ Échec du partage Gists" -ForegroundColor Red
00890:                     Write-Host "Erreur: $($result.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00891:                 }
00892:                 
00893:                 Write-Host ""
00894:                 Write-Host "Appuyez sur Entrée pour continuer..."
00895:                 Read-Host
00896:             }
00897:             
00898:             '3' {
00899:                 # OPTION 3: Fichiers locaux seulement
00900:                 $result = Generate-LocalFiles
00901:                 if ($result.success) {
00902:                     Write-Host ""
00903:                     Write-Host "✅ Génération locale réussie!" -ForegroundColor Green
00904:                     Write-Host "Fichier d'index: $($result.index_file)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00905:                     if ($result.share_files) {
00906:                         Write-Host "Fichiers partagés: $($result.share_files.Count)" -ForegroundColor Cyan
00907:                         foreach ($file in $result.share_files) {
00908:                             Write-Host "  - $file" -ForegroundColor Gray
00909:                         }
00910:                     }
00911:                     Write-Host "Nombre total de fichiers: $($result.file_count)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
00912:                 } else {
00913:                     Write-Host ""
00914:                     Write-Host "❌ Échec de la génération locale" -ForegroundColor Red
00915:                     Write-Host "Erreur: $($result.error)" -ForegroundColor Red
00916:                 }
00917:                 
00918:                 Write-Host ""
00919:                 Write-Host "Appuyez sur Entrée pour continuer..."
00920:                 Read-Host
00921:             }
00922:             
00923:             '4' {
00924:                 Write-Host "Au revoir!" -ForegroundColor Green
00925:                 exit 0
00926:             }
00927:             
00928:             default {
00929:                 Write-Host "Choix invalide!" -ForegroundColor Red
00930:                 Start-Sleep -Seconds 1
00931:             }
00932:         }
00933:     } while ($true)
00934: }
